[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Server-Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: untrusted or adversarial input leads to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnetwork requests to arbitrary destinations, potentially allowing exfiltration of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msensitive data or internal service discovery.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The call stack shows the HTTP connection is established within the XML parser’s[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity resolution [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXerces `XMLEntityManager` and `XMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The entry point is `XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps`, which [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvokes the SAX parser on parts of the XLSX file.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`POIFuzzer` → `POIXSSFFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m drives [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing of arbitrary input, but is not itself the root cause.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • External entity resolution in XML [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia HTTP[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is being exercised by the parser [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen handling document fragments or DTDs embedded in the spreadsheet.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Affected Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `org.apache.poi.xssf.extractor.XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand related XML parsing routines.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. XML parser configuration and entity resolver setup in the POI extractor [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g.,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhow external entities and DTDs are handled[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Any dependency or helper classes that may open HTTP connections during parsing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof workbook metadata.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Integration points where untrusted input controls the target URI for HTTP or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msocket connections.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReview of these areas will provide a holistic understanding of how untrusted Excel [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent can trigger external network calls and where controls or safeguards against[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSSRF should be applied.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call with POI’s `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand installs an entity resolver that ignores external references via [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XMLHelper::ignoreEntity`. However, the build now fails in the `poi-ooxml` module [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      SAXParser parser =[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35morg.apache.poi.util.XMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mparser.getXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.setEntityResolver[0m[1;39m([0m[39morg.apache.poi.util.XMLHelper::ignore[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEntity[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, new [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      with:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      XMLReader reader = [0m[1;35morg.apache.poi.util.XMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mreader.setContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mreader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Add the necessary imports at the top of the file:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import org.xml.sax.XMLReader;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import org.xml.sax.InputSource;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      import org.apache.poi.util.XMLHelper;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Maintain the same exception handling block:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mpart.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          XMLReader reader = [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mreader.setContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mreader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mParserConfigurationException | SAXException | IOException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m swallow[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Rationale:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is a public API that internally:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Configures the reader to ignore external entities via the private [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ignoreEntity`.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Enables secure-processing features to prevent XXE/SSRF.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Registers proper error handling.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This removes any need to directly reference the private `ignoreEntity` method [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand avoids compilation errors.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Parsing via `XMLReader` and `InputSource` preserves the existing [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent-handling logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExtendedPropertiesHandler`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without altering its [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msemantics.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigations:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The change does not alter the behavior of `ExtendedPropertiesHandler`; it only[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges how parsing is invoked.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing tests and fuzzer harnesses that rely on the SSEF fix will [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to work, as entity resolution is still disabled.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No modifications are made to external libraries, harness code, or other [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mutility classes.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Broader Consistency:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Audit other XML parsing entry points [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., in `getText` or other event-based [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextractors[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to ensure they also use `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` where appropriate. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis patch focuses on `getExtendedProps` but the pattern should be applied [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproject-wide.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
